1. **CSI node plugin client** - The gRPC client that communicates with the CSI driver node plugin
2. **CSI volume attach/detach controller** - The controller that manages volume attachment/detachment
3. **CSI volume provisioner** - The provisioner that creates/deletes volumes
4. **PersistentVolume controller that bridges CSI operations to the core storage API**

Let me categorize the files:

### CSI Node Plugin Client (gRPC client to CSI driver)
- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_client.go` - The main CSI gRPC client interface and implementation (NodePublishVolume, NodeUnpublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, NodeUnstageVolume, NodeGetInfo, etc.)
- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_plugin.go` - The CSI plugin (VolumePlugin implementation, RegistrationHandler for CSI driver registration)
- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_mounter.go` - CSI mounter (implements volume.Mounter, calls NodePublishVolume/NodeUnpublishVolume/NodeStageVolume/NodeUnstageVolume)
- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_attacher.go` - CSI attacher (implements volume.Attacher/Detacher, manages VolumeAttachment objects)
- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_block.go` - CSI block volume support
- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_drivers_store.go` - CSI drivers store (in-memory store of registered CSI drivers)
- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_metrics.go` - CSI metrics provider
- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_util.go` - CSI utilities
- `pkg/volume/csi/expander.go` - CSI volume expansion (NodeExpand)
- `pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go` - Node info manager (manages CSINode objects)

### CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller
- `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go` - The main attach/detach controller
- `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/util/util.go` - Utilities for attach/detach with C
